   18 : savemesh (Th, "results/mesh_initial.msh" );
   19 : while(stopmesh > tolmesh && ii < maxit){
   20 : 	jj = 0;
   21 : 
   22 : 	// Power penalty law
   23 : 	if(pen) q = qmax - 2 * exp(- ii / 2.);
   24 : 	else q = qmax;
   25 : 
   26 : 	IPOPT(J, gradJ, ipC, ipGradC, v[],
   27 : 	  lb  = xlb[], ub  = xub[],
   28 : 	 	  clb = clb  , cub = cub  ,
   29 : 	  checkindex = 1, structjacc = [gvi,gvj],
   30 : 	    maxiter = IPOPTmaxiter + 100 * (ii == 0), warmstart = ii,
   31 : 	  lm = lm, uz = uz[], lz = lz[], tol=  IPOPTtol
   32 : 	  );
   33 : 
   34 : 	// Helmholtz filter
   35 : 	if(helm && ii != maxit - 1){
   36 : 		solve helmholtz(vHelm, psi) = int2d(Th)(radius * (dx(vHelm) * dx(psi) + dy(vHelm) * dy(psi)))
   37 : 		                              + int2d(Th)(vHelm * psi)
   38 : 		                              - int2d(Th)(v * psi);
   39 : 		plot(v,  wait = 0, fill = 1, value = 1, ps = "results/" + ii + "_density_preHelm.ps", cmm = "Density preHelm " + ii);
   40 : 		plot(vHelm, wait = 0, fill = 1, value = 1, ps = "results/" + ii + "_density_postHelm.ps", cmm = "Density postHelm " + ii);
   41 : 		v = vHelm;
   42 : 	}
   43 : 
   44 : 	// Mesh filter
   45 : 	if(meshad && ii >= 4 && ii != maxit - 1){
   46 : 	  maxsK = 1;
   47 : 	  ntold = Th.nt;
   48 : 	  makemetrica(tau);
   49 : 		Th = adaptmesh(Th, metric = [m11[],m12[],m22[]], nbvx = 12000, periodic = [[2,y],[4,y],[1,x],[3,x]]);
   50 : 		savemesh (Th, "results/" + ii + "_mesh.msh" );
   51 : 		plot(Th, wait = 0, cmm="New mesh");
   52 : 		cout << "maxsK = " << maxsK << endl;
   53 : 	}
   54 : 
   55 : 	// Heaviside filter
   56 : 	if(heav && ii != maxit - 1){
   57 :     plot(v,  wait = 0, fill = 1, value = 1, ps = "results/" + ii + "_density_preHeav.ps", cmm = "Density preHeav " + ii);
   58 : 		real betaH = 10*(ii < 19) + 7*(ii == 19);
   59 : 		vHeav = 0.5 + tanh(betaH*(v-0.5))/(2*tanh(0.5*betaH));
   60 :     plot(vHeav, wait = 0, fill = 1, value = 1, ps = "results/" + ii + "_density_postHeav.ps", cmm = "Density postHeav " +ii);
   61 :     v = vHeav;
   62 : 	}
   63 : 
   64 : 	// Sigmund filter
   65 : 	if(sig && ii != maxit - 1){
   66 : 		real beta = beta0 + betaincr * ii;
   67 : 		real eta = eta0 + etaincr * ii;
   68 : 		plot(v,  wait = 0, fill = 1, value = 1, ps = "results/" + ii + "_density_preSig.ps", cmm = "Density preSig " + ii);
   69 : 		vSig = (1-xlb) * (tanh(beta * eta) + tanh(beta * (v - xlb - eta)))
   70 : 		               / (tanh(beta * eta) + tanh(beta * (1 - xlb - eta))) + xlb;
   71 : 		plot(vSig, wait = 0, fill = 1, value = 1, ps = "results/" + ii + "_density_postSig.ps", cmm = "Density postSig " + ii);
   72 : 		v = vSig;
   73 : 	}
   74 : 
   75 :   // Mesh projection
   76 :   if(meshad && ii >= 4 && ii != maxit - 1){
   77 :   	v = v;
   78 :   	xlb = xlb;
   79 :   	xub = xub;
   80 :   	gvi = gvi;
   81 :   	gvj = 0:Xhp.ndof-1;
   82 :   	lz = lz;
   83 :   	uz = uz;
   84 :   	m11 = m11;
   85 :   	m12 = m12;
   86 :   	m22 = m22;
   87 : 
   88 :   	stopmesh = abs(Th.nt - real(ntold))/ntold;
   89 :   }
   90 : 
   91 : 	ii += 1;
   92 : 
   93 : 	cout << "Iteration " << ii << ", Mesh error = " << stopmesh << endl;
   94 : 
   95 : 	{ofstream fout("results/" + ii + "_density.txt");	fout << v[];}
   96 : 
   97 : 	plot(v,  wait = 0, fill = 1, value = 1, ps = "results/" + ii + "_density.ps", cmm = "Density "+ii);
   98 : 	savevtk("results/" + ii + "_density.vtk", Th, v, dataname = "Density", order = ffordervel);
   99 : }
  100 : 
  101 : cout << Th.nt << endl;
  102 : 
  103 : plot(v,  wait = 0, fill = 1, value = 1, ps = "results/final_density.ps", cmm = "Final Density");
  104 :  sizestack + 1024 =359456  ( 358432 )

  -- Square mesh : nb vertices  =961 ,  nb triangles = 1800 ,  nb boundary edges 120
